Free Talk

A Laughable Matter by Haike

A: You have lunch at C Restaurant every day. How is their food? Is it cooked well?

B: The cooking is not bad. But they treat the chickens and ducks too well. It seems unfair to the general diners.

A: What's going on?

B: They raise chickens and ducks and can't bear to kill them when they are young. They only kill them when they are old. So their mustard chicken and braised duck are all highly respected elders.

A's Wife: My husband is really a blunderer. He is very careless about everything.

B's Wife: How careless?

A's Wife: Just look at the buttons on his clothes. They often fall off. I sew one on, and another one falls off.

B's Wife (shaking her head): Maybe you used too little thread when you sewed them on. Maybe you didn't sew them on very firmly.

A's Wife (shaking her head): Huh. That's none of my business. He sews them on himself.

A: What's in your little bag?

B: It's a poison.

A (feigning surprise): Ah. You bought poison. What for?

B: Don't be scared. It's a rat poison. Rats die as soon as they eat it.

A: Ah. I see. So you're tired of living. You're preparing to commit suicide.

The Wusheng Pass Tunnel on the Pinghan Railway by Tan Shenyu

Wusheng Pass belongs to Yingshan County, Hubei Province, bordering Henan. The terrain is mountainous and strategically important. When the Pinghan Railway was built during the late Qing Dynasty, due to the height of the mountains making it difficult to level, a tunnel was dug through them. The tunnel is more than sixteen li long, and it takes fifteen minutes for a train to pass through. Every traveler who has traveled on the Pinghan Railway knows about the Wusheng Pass tunnel. However, the tunnel was originally built to facilitate transportation, but who would have known that countless innocent people would die unjustly within it? Since the founding of the Republic of China, wars have been frequent, and the people in the war zones have suffered the most. In order to escape to other places, many find it convenient to take trains. However, during wartime, the railway is too busy transporting military vehicles to have time for passenger trains. Therefore, every train station is filled with refugees waiting for trains. Whenever a military train passes by, they rush to get on board. However, the train cars cannot possibly accommodate them all. Therefore, the weak cry and hate, while the strong climb onto the roof of the train. Because of their eagerness to escape, they do not listen to the strict prohibitions of the armed police (the train stations on the Pinghan Railway do not have fences and can be entered and exited freely, unlike the Jinghu Railway which is slightly more orderly, so the police cannot really prevent them). The tops of the train cars are often rounded and slippery. Due to the vibrations while the train is moving, very few manage to stay on. Furthermore, the Wusheng Pass tunnel was artificially constructed and is naturally not very high. It can only accommodate the body of the train. Nothing can be added on top of the train. Therefore, when the train arrives at Wusheng Pass, the refugees on the roof of the train are unaware of the danger of the tunnel. Those sitting on it will immediately hit the rocks on top of the tunnel and fall down. If they are not killed by the impact, they will certainly be crushed by the train.

China's Most Expensive Book by Pan Shizhu

A Book Worth One Hundred Thousand Yuan

The Collected Works of Han Changli and Liu Hedong of the Shicai Hall are one of the few surviving Song Dynasty editions. They have always been valued by collectors. The paper used by the Shicai Hall is of even texture and has been soaked in pepper water, so it does not suffer from insect damage even after hundreds of years. Moreover, the characters are engraved with a Tang Dynasty flavor, making it even more beloved. Currently, the Han collection is with the Yang family of Haiyuan Pavilion, while the Liu collection is with Pan Mingxun, a Cantonese in Shanghai. Last year, the descendants of the Yang family transported twenty-six fine editions from Haiyuan Pavilion to Tianjin, and the Han collection was among them, with the intention of selling them. Pan, in order to complete the collection and not wanting the precious book to fall into the hands of the Japanese, contacted the descendants of the Yang family to purchase the Han collection. However, the Yang family said they would not sell it for less than one hundred thousand yuan, as the value of the book is truly commensurate with the price. Currently, negotiations have stalled due to the excessive price difference. It is unknown whether the book has been sold. It is hoped that it does not fall into the hands of the Japanese, which would be fortunate. There was once a rumor that someone intended to purchase all twenty-six editions for two hundred thousand yuan to preserve China's national essence. The intention is good, but I fear it is not so easy. (Que Chou)

During the campaign against Feng in the eighteenth year of the Republic, a refugee named Liu from Henan, with his entire family of five, wanted to escape to Hankou to avoid the war. They climbed onto the roof of a military vehicle at Xinyang Station. When the train reached Wusheng Pass, three of the five family members hit the rocks in the tunnel and fell down. Only an old man of about fifty or sixty years old and his granddaughter of about ten years old escaped this calamity because they were lying flat on the roof of the train. Otherwise, they would have perished as well. Many people in Henan and Hubei can tell this story. I used to serve in the military and also worked on the front lines during the campaign against Tang. After the victory, I returned to Wuhan by train with the troops. When passing through Wusheng Pass, I wanted to see the condition of the tunnel, so I brought a flashlight with me. When the train first entered the tunnel (at this time it was daytime), the train car was filled with smoke, which was the gas emitted from the locomotive. After entering the tunnel, it immediately became a world of darkness. You could not even see the person across from you. Then, I smelled a foul odor. So, I shined the flashlight out the train window. What I saw were piles of skeletons with severed heads and broken limbs. The foul odor came from corpses that had not been rotting for long. Although no one has investigated the number, in that brief moment, I saw more than ten bodies. So, over the years, how many innocent people seeking refuge from war have been buried in this tunnel? Alas! (Bu Shou Chou)

Records of Bandit Troubles in Jiangxi Province Zheng

In recent years, the banditry in Hunan and Jiangxi has been unprecedented. Of the seventy-plus counties in Jiangxi Province, the provincial government's orders can only reach a dozen or so. The trampling and poisoning suffered by the people are truly indescribable. A friend recently came from Jiangxi and told me a few things. So, I took up a pen to record them.

▲Throwing Human Heads in Trenches: The only policy of the bandits is to kill and burn. Therefore, there is a special team responsible for killing. Occasionally, when confronting the army, they throw hundreds of human heads at the opposing side. The army is invariably horrified when they see this. Their cruelty is such.

▲Zhang Hui Met a Tragic End: Zhang Huizan, the commander of the Nanchang Garrison and division commander, was very talented and resourceful. The preservation of the provincial capital was mostly due to Zhang's efforts. However, recently, Zhang led his troops on an expedition and encountered a group of refugees. When asked, they said they had escaped from the bandits' den. When asked about the situation of the bandits, they all said that the bandits were weak and that if they were pursued victoriously, it would not be difficult to annihilate them in one fell swoop. Zhang believed them to be true. So, he personally led the remaining soldiers of his battalion to advance. Who knew that the bandits had lured them deep into the territory and then surrounded them? Zhang and two brigade commanders were captured. Only then did he realize that the refugees were all bandits. After the bandits captured Zhang, they subjected him to a so-called people's public trial. As a result, he was brutally disemboweled, and the provincial capital became even more precarious.

▲Mines Flooded: A friend operated a coal mine. The income from production each year was just enough to maintain it. However, as the bandits' power expanded, the mine was also occupied by the bandits. Later, they flooded it with water, saying, "Those who own mines must be rich people. We must destroy them." Thus, this mine worth hundreds of thousands of yuan was also sacrificed.

▲Family Massacred: A villager had four sons. One day, the villager was taken away by the bandits and sentenced to death. Upon hearing the news, the four sons went to the bandits' lair and said, "Our father is old. Please choose one of us four to replace him." The bandits said, "Good. Since you are all not afraid of death, then all of you can be executed." Thus, they were all killed together. Alas! What human tragedy is greater than this?

Parisian Tales (23) Six Once Lived in Paris

The most famous thing in the botanical garden is its labyrinth (Jabyrinthe) and science museum. The labyrinth is very cleverly constructed, making it difficult for people to find their way out after entering. The science museum is divided into several parts, including zoology, geology, mineralogy, etc. The specimens collected inside are extremely rich, and there are many rare things that cannot be seen elsewhere.

The botanical garden was founded in 1626, but the facilities were very simple before. It was not until the great naturalist and writer Buffon came to be the administrator that it was expanded to its current form. Buffon managed the botanical garden for nearly fifty years (1739-1788). He devoted almost all of his energy to his masterpiece "Natural History" (HistoireNaturelle) and this botanical garden. Now there is a bronze statue of him in the garden, and the house he used to live in is still preserved.

Every time I take a walk in the botanical garden, I often think back to when I was studying in Japan a few years ago, when I often went to the Koishikawa Botanical Garden in Tokyo. I love the scenery of the Koishikawa Botanical Garden, but the Koishikawa Botanical Garden does not have such a rich science museum as the Paris Botanical Garden. Among the several botanical gardens I have seen in Europe, I feel that the botanical garden in the capital of Belgium is very similar to the Paris Botanical Garden. But the size of the Belgian botanical garden is much smaller than that of the Paris Botanical Garden. Our country has plenty of open space, and the collection of plant specimens is ultimately easier than other scientific specimens. I hope that when I return to China in the future, I will be able to see a very beautiful botanical garden in our capital, with a very large natural history museum attached to it.

Review of the Musical "Where is He Gone?" by Huang Hua

Opera is popular in Western countries. This kind of opera does not only focus on singing and dancing, but also puts a lot of effort into the depiction of the plot. Looking back at the opera world in our country, due to its young qualifications and insufficient funds, it ends up being ambitious but unable to achieve its goals.

Newspapers have published that the Plum Blossom Opera Troupe has newly compiled a non-war opera called "Where is He Gone?", which is being performed at the Central, New Central, and Samsung theaters. As an attempt at opera, I went to see it. Examining its intention, it is generally about a conscript bidding farewell to his wife to go to war, and after a year, he returns seriously injured, only to find that his family is broken and his wife is dead. The last year's person is gone. It is set off by wild geese flying in formation when the husband and wife are separated, singing and dancing on the left and right, expressing that when humanity is inevitable, there will eventually be a day of separation, and we who live together day and night will never be separated by war. People are not as good as birds. The idea is still good. When the war breaks out, the people flee to avoid disaster, and there are many interjections. The husband calls his wife, the daughter calls her mother, and the old Buddha woman holds the Guanyin statue and chants Amitabha, etc., which is not out of line. The comic part is that a soldier is alone and has no one to say goodbye to, so he holds a portrait of a beautiful woman to comfort himself. As a result, he abandons the painting and competes with others for a piece of bread. The performance is excessive, and the idea focuses on the bread problem, which does not seem to be nonsense. Ms. Zhang Xianlin, who plays the wife, can express a sorrowful feeling when singing, but she fails to be thoroughly convincing when still. Huang Hunjun's soldier's appearance is not bad. His singing is too low. He should study the highs and lows of pronunciation. Ms. Qian Zhongxiu, Xu Canying, Cai Yiming, Gong Qiuxia, Zhang Qi, and Weng Lanhun play three pairs of geese, and their singing and dancing are all interesting. It is said that the rehearsal took a day. During the war, the flashing lights and music are harmonious. A model airplane flies from the top of the theater to the stage. Due to the lighting arrangement, it does not feel annoying. However, this is just a gimmick. In a word, if this script is more carefully revised, it should have value. In the era of the budding of Chinese opera, our vision should be a little lower. I hope that Mr. Wei Yingbo and Cai Wenjin, who co-edited this play, will work hard to cultivate this bud, so that Chinese stage opera can gradually move towards the path of light.

To Mr. A and B: Thank you for your letter. Most of the points you mentioned are already in the planning stage. I look forward to your face-to-face instructions.

Chapter 17: The Art of Staying Young: Emerald Eyebrows and Painted Eyebrows, No Way to Extend Life: Golden Market and Fine Bones

After Hua Yuanchun had this pair of beloved people, although she had eternal life and was indestructible, she was a little overwhelmed. The other guests were a bit mediocre and unworthy of mention. Not to mention that she is temporarily attached to them and unwilling to marry. When people inquire about this pair of dragging objects, who would want to marry her? The money lent to her can never be recovered. Later, everyone discussed, saying it would be better to instigate her to go out of the pier. Now there are many girls going south to Beijing and Tianjin. Because the masters in the south go to Beijing to be officials, they naturally like the girls in the south and don't like the girls in the north. I heard that someone went and picked up three thousand yuan in one night. Not to mention touching her body, they didn't even touch her hand. The adults are very generous. Miss Six's skills are not bad. It's just that she's been nailed down by these two enemies. If she leaves Shanghai, she might make a big tip and come back. Now A Jin, the big-bellied man from Qingyutang, is coming to Shanghai to pick up the young ladies. Let's talk to him.

A Discussion on the Cause and Effect of the Rising Price of Broad Silver Dollars

The Shanghai port is commercially prosperous, and the residents are particularly affluent. Therefore, the demand for daily necessities is also greater than in other metropolitan areas. This time, the unusual rise in the price of broad silver dollars due to a shortage of goods, and the great impact on the people's livelihood, is a logical and inevitable fact. Moreover, the exchange shops are forcibly suppressing prices, causing residents to suffer even more. Few outside the industry know the reasons for the price increase. Therefore, after detailed interviews by reporters, the following cause and effect were obtained. According to past experience, the Shanghai port has always suffered from a glut of broad silver dollars, with supply exceeding demand in the market. Furthermore, shipments from Shantou and Xiamen continue to arrive. Therefore, at the cheapest time, the price has been more than 12 jiao per silver dollar. Last summer, the Dalian gang saw the Shanghai port's exchange rate rising and purchased shipments for export, ranging from 200,000 to 300,000 jiao per batch. This lasted for half a year, and the Shanghai port's current base was almost eroded by more than half. Those in the industry knew that this continuous collection would eventually lead to panic one day, so those with power competed to purchase and hoard them. Afterwards, market prices gradually increased, and the hoarders then sold them at good prices to other gangs, leading to a shortage of cash that everyone needed, and the circulation became tight. After the small exchange shops competed to suppress prices, and the hoarding and trading houses added to the manipulation, it coincided with the end of the lunar year. In the prosperous era of previous years, there were already such strong suppression measures. How much more so in the current time of shortage? As a result, the prices continued to rise, forming the current phenomenon. It is rumored that there may be further contractions in the future, and it is not known whether the price will be one silver dollar for ten jiao. The early market yesterday was 6 qian 8 fen and a half li, and the afternoon market was 6 qian 8 fen and 2 li, an increase of 3 li compared to the previous day. Transactions amounted to 125,000 jiao in the early market and 120,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Jiangnan small foreign silver dollars in the early market were 6 qian 7 fen and 4 li, and in the afternoon market, they were 6 qian 7 fen and 5 li, also with a slight increase of 1 or 2 li. Transactions amounted to 6,000 jiao in the early market and 7,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Steel dollars were lengthened by 500 wen, amounting to 356,500,000 wen, with over 30,000 strings traded.

Local News

Important Talk by Zhang Qun

▲Day and Night Bank Liquidation Incident

▲Municipal Government Decides to Take Responsibility

▲Each Factory First Sends Personnel for Inspection

▲Complete Inaccuracy of Being Sent to Sichuan

Our reporter interviewed Mayor Zhang Qun at the Municipal Government yesterday to inquire about the aftermath of the Day and Night Bank liquidation case and various issues such as business tax. The following is a summary of his remarks.

▲Day and Night Bank Regarding the liquidation of the Day and Night Bank and the Great World Amusement Savings Department, Zhang said that most of the depositors are laborers and women, which has a huge impact on the livelihood of the common people. The Ministry of Industry and the Municipal Government have repeatedly received appeals from creditors, requesting maintenance and handling. Recently, it has been heard that three or five depositors have committed suicide as a result, which is very pitiful. The Municipal Government cannot stand idly by. It has now decided to take responsibility for the handling and seek more benefits for the creditors. It is currently exchanging opinions with all parties and carefully discussing everything. It is expected that a direction can be determined in two or three days. The main points of the method are to gather all relevant parties for open consultations and stipulate methods for repaying debtors. Currently, the most difficult issue is the Gongfa Company and Huang Chujiu's private property, which are scattered in the Public Concession and the French Concession. If the French Concession handles it, its power only extends to the Great World and the Day and Night Bank headquarters. Moreover, once the stores are closed, the losses will be even greater, and the creditors will suffer even greater losses. In short, this move by the Municipal Government is entirely to seek benefits for the creditors, and I will do my best to ensure a perfect outcome.

▲Business Tax Rate Regarding the issue of business tax rates, Zhang said that the Municipal Finance Committee is currently conducting detailed research. After the decision is made, the Municipal Government will submit it to the Central Government for approval, hoping to obtain a fair disposition. As for the merchants in the concessions, they are also Chinese nationals and should have the obligation to pay taxes. The difficulty is that the concessions have already levied a license tax similar to business tax. This is currently being considered, and the merchants will not be subject to double taxation.

▲Inspection of Factories The Factory Law and the Implementing Regulations of the Factory Law have been resolved by the National Government meeting to be postponed until August 1. Mayor Zhang said yesterday that there are about one thousand several hundred factories in Shanghai, and several hundred of them do not comply with the Factory Law. The first step is to send personnel to investigate and inspect them one by one. Those who do not comply will find ways to reform and make full preparations in advance, so that there will be no more difficulties in the short term.

▲Yuan Liang's Resignation Public Security Bureau Chief Yuan Liang has submitted his resignation, and I have forwarded his resignation to the Central Government. The successor has been internally determined to be Mr. Chen Xizeng. I met with him yesterday, and he will officially take over after the Central Government issues an order.

▲Rumors of Going to Sichuan When the reporter asked whether the rumors that the Central Government intends to send the mayor to Sichuan to preside over Sichuan affairs were true, Zhang replied that there was no such thing. Although Sichuan is my hometown, I have been away from Sichuan for a long time and have many barriers. I am willing to offer opinions on Sichuan affairs but do not want to join the vortex. There are rumors that President Dai Jitao will go, but the Central Government has no such intention either. I have recently been working hard on the construction of the central area of the city, which will begin in May and be able to lay the foundation in July. I firmly believe that one person should focus on one thing to achieve some success. Even if the Central Government issues an order for promotion, I know that my talent and strength are insufficient and I will not dare to accept it.

Study Group on Various Industry Tax Regulations Holds Second Committee Meeting Yesterday

The Tax Regulation Study Committee of various industry guilds in this city held its second committee meeting yesterday. The committee members present were Ye Chunqiao, Xie Zhongle, Ge Yuanqing (represented by Ma Jiliang), Luo Qinghua, Shen Weiting, Cheng Youfu, Lin Zhangrong, Shao Baoxing, Wang Lianfang, Hu Juewen, Zhao Xiaolin, and more than ten others. Luo Qinghua served as chairman, and Sun Mingqi was the recorder. The meeting began with the usual formalities. First, the chairman gave a report, and then discussions began. The resolutions are recorded as follows: (1) Regarding the motion submitted by He Yinsheng, a representative of the candle industry, at the second general meeting of various industries, requesting that the competent authorities handle business tax matters with simplicity and efficiency when implementing them, it was resolved to present the matter to the provincial finance departments for their attention. (2) Regarding the letters from the Western clothing industry, embroidery industry, foil industry, ginseng and bird's nest industry, paint industry, cosmetics industry, ham industry, candle industry, silk and satin industry, and copper and tin industry, requesting to reduce business tax rates, it was resolved to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance of the National Government based on the opinions of various industries. It was requested that the business tax rates in various provinces and cities not exceed two per thousand, except where the government has other regulations below two per thousand. The wholesale part should still be taxed at one-quarter. The collection method should follow the plan proposed by Anhui Province and be based on the proportion of business volume. (3) Regarding how to stipulate the regular meeting date of this committee, it was resolved to hold a meeting every Wednesday at 2:00 PM. If necessary, temporary meetings will be convened. The remaining matters were brief. Also, the committee sent a document to the Municipal Executive Committee and letters to various members of the Municipal Finance Discussion Committee who are related to the business community. The original texts are recorded below:

▲Document Presented to the Municipal Executive Committee: Presenting the matter of implementing business tax in this city, which is related to increasing the burden on citizens, requesting special attention and hoping for verification to benefit people's livelihood. It is noted that after the abolition of likin, using consolidated tax and special tax to compensate for central government losses, and using business tax to compensate for local government losses, was the fundamental plan decided by the likin abolition conference. The level of business tax rates in various provinces and cities should comply with the guidelines promulgated by the Executive Yuan, taking into account the actual losses suffered by the province or city due to the abolition of likin to determine the tax rate, which is not an easy conclusion. However, this city has never had likin revenue. This time, the explicit abolition of likin has not resulted in any losses. It should not follow the example of other provinces and implement business tax. If, as reported in the newspapers in recent days, the business tax planned by the Finance Bureau is purely an unexpected income, then the hope of merchants and people for the abolition of likin to reduce the burden, and the local government's increase in income due to the abolition of likin, would not be the central government's intention to benefit merchants and people, nor would it be consistent with the original intention of the likin abolition policy. Moreover, the situation in this city is special, with the separation of concessions and the presence of foreign capital, which has not yet achieved the goal of universality and equality. The harm caused will be ten times greater than the abuses of likin. This association is an organization composed of more than one hundred industry guilds, and this matter concerns their vital interests. They dare to present this appeal, hoping that your committee will pay special attention to eliminate business difficulties and benefit people's livelihood, which would be a great virtue. Respectfully submitted.

▲Letter to Discussion Committee Members: To gentlemen Qia Qing, Ji, Yan Song, Hui Jun, and Run Qing, it has often been heard that there is no taxation without representation. This is the golden rule of democratic countries and the initial foundation for the establishment of civil rights. After the National Government was established, it governed the country with the Three Principles of the People. All systems, both Chinese and foreign, ancient and modern, cannot be cited, so that the fundamental law has not yet been promulgated. Taking the city as an example, although the municipal system has been explicitly promulgated, the Municipal Council, which represents the citizens, has not yet been organized according to law. Therefore, there is no formal review and approval body for the municipal tax system, budget, and final accounts, which increase the burden on the people. For the sake of collecting opinions and benefiting widely, the municipal finance authorities have organized a Finance Discussion Committee. Those who are extended invitations are either financial experts or business leaders, and their positions are voluntary. They are not like the members of the Construction Discussion Committee, who can receive a monthly allowance of one hundred yuan. Since the establishment of the Municipal Finance Discussion Committee, the most well-known achievements to the citizens are the borrowing of rental fees and the raising of municipal public bonds, all for the purpose of supporting the progress of municipal construction. Their enthusiasm is admirable. Compared with the former Shanghai Special Municipal Council's discussion of increasing rental donations and deciding to reduce the discount, and the discussion of issuing municipal bonds and deciding to postpone the handling, one is passive and the other is active, which are truly incomparable. Recently, this city plans to implement business tax, and your committee has conducted two discussions, and the collection regulations and implementation rules have been initially passed. As for the tax rate issue, according to the newspaper report on the 2nd of this month, Chairman Wang Xiaolai stated that he will ask various industries to submit their opinions on the tax rate, and the committee will discuss them based on the submissions from various industries, form a draft, and then submit it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to convene a general meeting of representatives from various industries, which will then be reported to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation. This shows that you are concerned about the pain of various industries and the hardships of business. (1) Compared with the financial authorities of Jiangsu Province, who independently formulate without soliciting opinions from merchants and people, it is a hundred times better. Compared with the financial authorities of Zhejiang Province, who only invited a few representatives to pass important cases concerning the burden on the people, and failed to distinguish between luxury and non-luxury goods in detail, they must heavily tax all major products to increase revenue, regardless of whether they should be maintained and how their current situation is declining. As a result, the draft was passed first, and the merchants and people cried out later, accusing and blaming each other on the road. You must have seen the details in the newspapers. I hope that you will learn from the past and avoid repeating the same mistakes, understand the wishes of merchants and people, and only follow the regulations of the central government to use special tax and consolidated tax to compensate for the central government's losses due to the abolition of likin, and use business tax to compensate for the local government's losses due to the abolition of likin. The first step is to ask the municipal finance authorities to publicly announce the amount of losses suffered by this city due to the abolition of likin as the sole criterion for discussing the tax rate. The second step is if the municipal finance authorities believe that construction requires funding, and business tax has already been implemented in various provinces, it would not be cruel to take it in this city. Then, when issuing municipal public bonds in the past, it was also designated for municipal construction. Now that the public bonds have been raised in full, and the construction achievements may be considerable, it is also requested to report to the municipal government to announce the construction projects undertaken by using public bonds to the citizens, so that the citizens can also be happy to support the promotion of new taxes, which will be easily effective. The third step is that the Chinese and concession boundaries must be uniformly implemented, and Chinese and foreign shops should be treated equally. Since the mayor has already said it, you should have a good understanding of it and promote its realization. Furthermore, the citizen representative agency has a fixed organization according to law. Then, you are acting as financial discussion committee members in your current capacity as natural persons. Even if you can speak for merchants and people and think for citizens, your words will not be legitimate if your name is not correct. It is not easy to be understood by citizens. Moreover, there are administrative authorities in the committee, and it is difficult to find people who do not violate their conscience and speak frankly, as Ji An advocated. The intention of this association is to ask you to report to the municipal government authorities to quickly organize the municipal council according to law. If direct elections by citizens are still difficult, then follow the National Assembly election law and have various legal groups elect them separately. If the official representative agency of citizens is established as soon as possible, it will be able to exercise its legally assigned powers in the council, and you can also avoid the blame for perfection. This is a win-win situation. I respectfully present my sincerity, hoping that you will take it into consideration and wish you all the best.

Xu Yongzuo Discusses Business Tax Issues

The Municipal Government Finance Bureau has repeatedly convened the Finance Discussion Committee to discuss the method of handling business tax in this city. The Tax Regulation Research Association of various industries in this city has sent letters to Finance Minister Song and Finance Discussion Committee members Pan Xulun and Xu Yongzuo to express their opinions. Yesterday, reporters from various newspapers specially visited accountant Xu to inquire about the details. He provided the following answers: (Question) It was reported in the newspapers a few days ago that the Finance Discussion Committee had passed the draft of the business tax collection regulations and implementation rules. Is this true? (Answer) The committee is an advisory body to the Finance Bureau. Although it has revised and passed the draft regulations, whether they will be implemented according to these regulations still depends on the Finance Bureau, the Municipal Government, and the Central Government for approval. (Question) The business tax rates in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are considered too high by all industries. How is the tax rate in this city compared to Jiangsu and Zhejiang? (Answer) The committee is currently only discussing the articles of the business tax regulations and has not yet talked about the numbers of the tax rate. In the future, it will be based on the Ministry's Business Tax Outline and Supplementary Measures, and there is no need to follow the tax rates set by Jiangsu and Zhejiang. (Question) When discussing the business tax issue in Zhejiang Province, experts were invited to participate. Did you attend at that time? (Answer) I am in Shanghai and have many affairs. I have never been invited to participate in Zhejiang Province, so I have not heard about the discussion. (Question) You must have a good understanding of the business tax issue. What are your opinions on the business tax method in this city? (Answer) I have been invited by various ministries and departments to discuss industrial and commercial tax systems and other laws and regulations, and I have always focused on being suitable for the national conditions and do not want to make unrealistic talk. I am ashamed that I have not deeply studied the various theories and examples of business tax in various countries, so when discussing the business tax method in this city, I should especially take into account the domestic environment as a prerequisite. The industry and commerce in our country are not yet developed, and the tax rate burden should be reduced. (Question) What is your opinion on the letter sent to you by the Tax Regulation Research Association of various industries? (Answer) The statements in the letter from the association that were published in the newspapers are actually due to misunderstandings, but I have not yet received the letter. I have already sent a letter to clarify, "Respected Sirs, I recently read in the newspaper that your association sent a letter to Mr. Pan Xulun and me, stating that when Zhejiang Province discussed the business tax rate, a certain expert attended the meeting and often compared it with the business tax rate in foreign countries. The business tax rate in Jiangsu is based on Zhejiang. The efforts of the chambers of commerce in the sixty counties of Jiangsu are indirectly due to the expert. The Shanghai business tax case is in preparation, and you are all members of the Municipal Finance Bureau Finance Discussion Committee. Since Jiangsu and Zhejiang have made mistakes in the past, this city should prevent repeating the same mistakes and offer good advice as a good medicine. I have not yet received this letter, but it has already been disclosed in the newspaper, which is very suspicious. I have many affairs in Shanghai and have never been invited by Zhejiang Province to go to Hangzhou to discuss the business tax case, so I have not heard about the discussion of the tax rate. Moreover, I have been invited by various ministries and departments in the past to discuss industrial and commercial tax systems and other laws and regulations, all based on the principle of being suitable for the national conditions and not making unrealistic talk. This time, when discussing the business tax issue in this city, I believe that I have not studied the theories and examples of business tax in various countries, and considering that the industry and commerce in our country are not yet developed, I should especially take into account the domestic environment and reduce the burden on various industries. The letter published in the newspaper is obviously due to misunderstandings. I am afraid that it will confuse the hearing, so I specially send this letter to you for your review to eliminate misunderstandings. Sincerely, to the Tax Regulation Research Association of various industry guilds in Shanghai, February 5, 20th year."

Chen Shaokuan Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

▲Discussed the Recent Situation of the Navy

According to the Guowen News Agency, Chen Shaokuan, the Vice Minister of the Navy and Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning. The reporter visited him at the shipyard in the afternoon and asked about the recent situation of the navy. He talked about the following:

▲Planning Maritime Rights: Mr. Chen said that foreign fishing boats have repeatedly invaded our country's coastal areas to fish, so determining territorial sea rights is an urgent matter. The day before yesterday, the government ordered the Ministry of Navy to work with the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Interior to plan the scope of the territorial sea. It has been drafted and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review. The order has not yet been received today. The regulations are roughly the same as those of other countries. The area within three miles of the coast (excluding beaches and sand beaches where water does not reach) is the territorial sea. Unless it is a port of entry, foreign ships are not allowed to invade. Then, send ships to patrol. Not only will sovereignty not be spilled out, but the fishing industry will also be revitalized. The plan is awaiting the approval of the Yuan order before it can be implemented, so this matter is in progress and cannot be delayed.

▲Yangtze River Defense: The Yangtze River defense is very solid. There are almost no bandits along the riverbanks. Even if there are small groups of bandits, they are all in the inland areas along the river. Although bandits were found in Chenglingji the day before yesterday, they were dispersed by Ren Sheng's suppression. At present, major ports along the river, from Yichang to the capital, have warships stationed. Jiang Zhen ship is stationed in Hankou, Jiang Kun ship in Jianli, Gong Sheng ship in Yuezhou, Jiang Xi ship in Xindi, Chu Qian and Yong Sui ships in Jiujiang, Jiang Yuan ship in Wuxue, Xian Ning ship in Hukou, Wei Sheng ship in Anqing, Chu You ship in Nanjing, and eight torpedo ships, such as Hu Peng, Hu Ying, and Hu Ji, which are exercising in Baguazhou.

▲Establishing a School in Xiangshan: Xiangshan is indeed a natural harbor. The Ministry of Navy has decided to set up a naval school there first. The estimated cost is 200,000 to 300,000 yuan. As soon as the construction plan is drafted, it will begin. The Ministry of Navy has sent the Tong Ji training ship there to plan. In the future, students will be admitted through examinations, not by sending them from various ships. The number of students will probably be 300. As for the port construction, this matter is significant, and the cost is not 100,000 or 200,000 yuan. Therefore, the saying that Xiangshan is actively building the port is not yet the time, let alone when there are no plans or funds.

▲Renovating Warships: The renovation of the abandoned Da An warship has been completed, and it has been renamed Da Tong. Following the renovation of this ship, there is still Jian Wei. It is said that the Jian Wei project is expected to be completed in three months, and it can be completed together with the new Yi Xian ship. The old name of Jian Wei has been decided not to be used, and the new name has been set as Zi Qiang. As for the Min Sheng warship, which is currently under construction, half of the project has been built and will be launched at the end of March or the beginning of April this year. The rumor that the Navy is purchasing new ships from abroad is false because there is no such thing in the Ministry of Navy.

Chinese Shipping Industry Opposes Sino-American Joint Shipping

▲Serious Expression Will Be Made Within Days

According to sources in the shipping industry yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company plans to jointly run Sino-American shipping with the American Dollar Steamship Company, providing a large number of ships for the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to use and registering with the Chinese government. Everything is generally controlled by the Chinese. All matters are being actively carried out in recent days. The shipping industry in this port is very shocked upon hearing the news. The initial rhetoric is very pleasant to the ear. For example, Sino-American joint shipping can recover shipping rights and various slogans, but it will ultimately lead to the bankruptcy of the Chinese shipping industry. Once implemented, it will be like letting wolves into the house. It is said that a serious expression will be made within days.

▲Fog Blocks Various Ships from Entering the Port: Up to forty ships were blocked by the heavy fog outside Wusong this time. The fog dispersed by noon yesterday, and the blocked merchant ships began to arrive in Shanghai one after another. The Tai Gu Ning Shao's Shanghai-Ningbo ship was delayed until 3:00 PM. The remaining Yangtze River and coastal ships arrived in Shanghai within three, four, or five hours, reaching twenty-eight ships. Some ships that were unable to arrive in Shanghai will arrive in Shanghai today.

▲Gong He Ship Runs Aground: The Jardine Matheson Yangtze River ship Gong He ran aground near Datong this time when sailing downstream from Hankou due to the receding river water and fog. Yesterday, the company received a wireless from Gong He saying that after Gong He ran aground, it had reversed out of the shoal during high tide. It had passed Wuhu at 1:00 PM and could reach Shanghai today.

British Merchant Ship Occupies Zhenjiang Water Surface Rights

▲China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Negotiates with Jardine Matheson

Guo Yanmo, the director of the Zhenjiang branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, presented to General Manager Li Zhonggong yesterday, stating that the Zhenjiang branch's lotus pond wharf ship surface property, which is owned by the bureau, is occupied by a British ship. Negotiations have been requested repeatedly, but the wharf ship is still docked as usual, which has a great impact on the bureau's business economy. It is not just the encroachment of the bureau's property. The export cargo loading in Zhenjiang Port is already light. If the ships can dock at the wharf all year round, it may be possible to compete slightly. Moreover, the sand beaches along the river are unpredictable with the rising and falling tides. Except for the location of the Nisshin wharf ship, the water depth of the lotus pond bureau property is the deepest. If the bureau's wharf ship is moved, it will not be able to dock for almost half of the year. When the water is shallow in winter, small ships are rented to tow iron barges to load and unload passengers and goods, which is cumbersome and time-consuming. When there is a lot of cargo, wooden barges must be hired, which is a loss for the bureau and inconvenient for the passengers. Considering the situation, the relocation of the wharf cannot be delayed. The lotus pond river surface has been occupied by the Jardine Matheson wharf ship. Unless it is negotiated to move back quickly, the bureau's wharf ship cannot be moved. It is reasonable to submit this to your seat and urgently negotiate. General Manager Li believes that the river surface property should not be occupied by foreign ships. Yesterday, he sent a letter to Jardine Matheson, ordering them to return it soon. Otherwise, he will submit it to the central government for negotiation and order them to withdraw the wharf ship as soon as possible.

Shanghai-Ningbo Ship Escort Team Established Early

▲Board the Ship on the 20th of This Month

▲Determine the Number of Team Members

▲Recruitment of Escort Team: The addition of escort teams to the Shanghai-Ningbo ships has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, the three companies continued to meet and have agreed on the team members to be placed on each ship. They have been reduced again to eleven soldiers and one squad leader per ship. The military police will not be used. Instead, the three companies will recruit them. Thirty-six people will be recruited first. Yu Qiaqing and others have recruited them. After the uniforms are specified and the military equipment is requested, they will be sent to each ship to serve.

▲Request for Military Equipment: Yesterday, the three companies sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau requesting military equipment, stating that cases of pirates looting ships have been frequently seen recently. If precautions are not taken in advance, it is not enough to secure the safety of travelers. The method of pirates attempting to loot ships is generally to dress up as passengers and mix into each cabin. When the ship is in the middle of the journey, they hold firearms and gather together to monitor the crew and kidnap the passengers. They do whatever they want and loot as much as they want. After looting, they either force the crew to drive to the pirate den or the nearby coast, or the pirates drive away themselves. The crew is helpless, and the passengers are stunned. The prevention strategy is to have armed soldiers protect the ship to secure the safety of travelers and maintain the shipping industry. Our company has decided to form an escort team on the Shanghai-Ningbo route, with one captain and one vice-captain to supervise. Each ship will have one squad leader and eleven soldiers stationed on the ship. If any passengers are suspicious or if any firearms are found, they will be immediately sent to your bureau for punishment. If they are discovered midway, they will have the ability to resist. The bandits will not dare to try to board knowing that there is an armed escort team on the ship. At ordinary times, they will protect the passengers, and in case of an emergency, they will be prepared. The roster of soldiers will be reported separately for record. The firearms for the escort team added to our company's ships should be requested to be issued and collected by your bureau (omitted below).

▲Board the Ship Early: Yesterday, the three companies decided to send them to each ship to escort as soon as the firearms are collected. Since the passenger fare for Shanghai-Ningbo will be increased on the 18th, the escort soldiers will also be sent on the first ship in the lunar month of February. It is estimated that it will be implemented on the 20th of this month.

▲Reply to Various Tea Rooms: The tea room guilds of various ships expressed opposition to this case and requested to stop increasing the export cargo fare and passenger tickets. Yesterday, the three companies replied to the tea room guilds, stating that adding an escort team and adding passenger fares are the facilities that the business department should have, and it has been decided to implement them. The request to stop adding fares and for the crew to serve as team members cannot be approved.

▲ Representatives of Various Unions Express Their Views

▲ Willing to Accept Consolidation

Yesterday (the 4th), the Popular Training Committee of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters, in conjunction with the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, convened representatives of various established unions throughout the city at the Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs to hold talks on the issue of union consolidation. From the newspaper industry, Tang Haiquan, Dai Xengeng, and Chen Qingrong from the Newspaper Industry Union attended. From the publishing industry, Yang Youren, Wang Wenhua, and Ni Xiaoxian from the Commercial Press attended; Chen Longzhang, Zhang Ruyu, and Wan Pusheng from the Commercial General Affairs Office Workers Union; Wang Yongliang, Shen Shangfang, and Ma Wei from the Commercial Distribution Office Workers Union; Chen Yuesheng, Zhu Gongchui, and Chen Bowen from the Commercial Translation Office Workers Union, represented by Guo Yongxi and Zhang Shuye, attended the talks. In the afternoon, from the straw hat industry, Wang Yuxiang, Zhou Zhiqing, and Song Wenbiao from the Straw and Felt Hat Industry Union, represented by Gu Bingyuan and Wang Youmei, attended the talks. From the garment industry, Zhou Shangen from the Western Clothing Union and Cai Ziwen from the Garment Union, represented by Guo Yongxi and Zhang Shuye, attended the talks. After the chairman's report, representatives from each union expressed their opinions. They considered there to be no problem with merging into a district union. However, four difficulties were discovered during the talks: (1) Representatives from the Western Clothing and Garment Unions believed it was difficult to merge because their work skills are different. (2) The straw hat industry can only establish a Hunan District Union with only 150 members, and the collected membership fees cannot be maintained. (3) Special areas in the straw hat industry, and others, cannot organize district unions due to insufficient statutory numbers. If the capitalists in that area abuse the recruitment of apprentices, the Hunan District cannot restrict it. (4) Because the Lunar New Year is approaching for the straw hat industry, workers are returning to their hometowns, and it is impossible to convene a reorganization in the shortest possible time. The chairman personally instructed that the party and government organs should carefully review and handle the matter.

The Newspaper Industry Union and the Four Unions of the Commercial Press Hold Talks with the Bureau of Social Affairs

▲ Requesting Guarantee of Original Labor-Capital Contracts

Yesterday, the Newspaper Industry Union and the four unions of the Commercial Press were summoned by the Bureau of Social Affairs for talks. Chairman Guo Yongxi reported on the significance of reorganizing the union. Representatives of the Newspaper Industry Union stood up and (asked): After the union is reorganized, will the originally established labor-capital contract still be valid? (Answer): There is no problem with this point, because reorganization and contract are two different issues. (Question): This reorganization is based on the Union Law, and subsequent arbitrations will naturally be based on the Union Law. In that case, the entire labor-capital contract will be shaken. Taking the first article of the contract as an example, if the union has the right to represent all "workers," and the Union Law stipulates that "union members may withdraw from the union at any time, and the standards for handling labor disputes state that 'it is not allowed to stipulate that workers expelled from union membership must also be terminated from their jobs by the capitalists," then members may collude with the capitalists, or the capitalists may buy off members to undermine the organization. The union is bound by the law and cannot prevent it. Such a reorganization is equivalent to dissolution. (Answer): There is no need to worry about this. The Union Law has been implemented for a long time, and no such incidents have occurred. Reorganization may provide protection. (Question): Can you be responsible? (Answer): The scope of today's talks is limited to reorganization. The contract is another issue and is not convenient to answer. (Question): The original contract, agreed upon by both labor and capital, has been in effect for nearly four years. If it loses its protection after reorganization, our association will not dare to reorganize. (Answer): Representatives, do not use contract protection as an exchange condition for reorganization, nor think that a contractual relationship will arise after reorganization. If you do not reorganize, you are an illegal organization, and the contract has even less protection. It is better to reorganize and then submit a request for protection. (Question): Reorganization is not a problem in itself, as long as the contract is protected, it can be reorganized at any time. We hope that the Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs will clearly stipulate this. Chairman Guo (asked): The Union Law has been implemented for a long time. Why has it not been submitted for amendment? (Answer): All the unions in Shanghai have submitted documents four or five times and petitioned in Beijing two or three times, but to no avail. Representatives from the commercial and industrial sectors stood up successively to ask further questions: (1) The rights that our association has fought for four or five years will be lost once due to reorganization. Who wouldn't be heartbroken? (2) Comrade Wu Kaixian said when talking with our association that the labor-capital contract is not a problem. (3) It is necessary to ask the Party and government organs to clearly stipulate that "the labor-capital contract will never be changed due to reorganization," etc. The chairman accepted the opinions and forwarded them to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs, and announced them in the newspapers on the same day.

Silk Factory Trade Association Holds General Meeting Yesterday

▲ Several Important Cases Resolved

The Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association held a general meeting of all members at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than 100 people attended, including Huang Jin Chen, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Huiseng, Zhu Jing'an, and Zhang Peishen. Shen Huachen presided over the meeting, and the formalities were observed. First, the silk factory public debt case was discussed. The chairman reported on the circumstances of the case, stating that the public debt case had been approved by the Administrative Council but had not yet been announced and implemented. At a time when the business community is closing accounts, money is extremely tight, and factories urgently need funds to turn around. Vice Minister Zhang of Finance is currently in Shanghai, and representatives should be elected immediately to urge him in person. In addition to electing Wang Xiaolai, Shen Huachen, Huang Jinchen, Zhu Jing'an, Wu Shenbo, Zhang Yunsheng, Huang Jinfan, and Chu Huiseng, who are rescue committee experts and Shanghai representatives, Shi Xinsheng, Yu Shouchang, Sun Rongchang, Chen Mingshan, and Xu Yunjiang were also added. It was decided to gather at the Wei Cheng Company on Beijing Road at 2:30 PM today and go by car at 3:00 PM to the Central Bank building on the Bund to meet with Vice Minister Zhang of Finance in person and request that he urge the Yuan Department to issue the bonds quickly, and present a summary. Secondly, the silk factory business tax case was discussed. Chu Huiseng stood up and reported on the situation of the representatives who went to Beijing to visit the heads of the Legislative and Executive Yuan, as well as the ministers of finance and industry, and entertained the officials to discuss the situation. It was the consensus that factory silk is related to international trade and should not be treated the same as other luxury goods. It should be requested that the silk cocoon industry, which sells goods in the business tax rate table, be deleted and exempted from taxation. It was decided to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, etc., requesting permission to exempt business tax in order to maintain the silk industry. Thirdly, the dry cocoon special tax case was discussed. It was the consensus that the previous cocoon donation was eight yuan per hundred catties, plus various surcharges and local miscellaneous donations, for a total of only twelve yuan. Now, it has been changed to a special tax, which taxes ten yuan per hundred catties. On the surface, it seems to be reduced by two yuan, but in reality, adding various surcharges will cost about fifteen or sixteen yuan, which is a heavier burden for silk merchants and is difficult to comply with. It was decided that all silk factories would jointly stamp and submit a petition to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, etc., requesting complete reduction and exemption in order to lighten the burden and fund development. Fourthly, the Factory Law was discussed. Wang Xiaolai reported on the situation of going to Beijing to visit Chairman Jiang, etc., and requesting permission to extend the implementation date to August 1st. It was the consensus that the various articles of the Factory Law are too restrictive, and the industry has difficulty complying with them. It was decided to submit petitions to the Yuan Department, ordering them to revise them. Fifthly, the coal industry sent a letter requesting an increase in the package price. The chairman reported that various coal companies had repeatedly sent letters stating that the current coal price is soaring, the source is not sustainable, and the inventory is getting thinner. They requested that the package price for each factory be increased by eight cents per car (the original price was 30 cents per silk car). It was decided to send a letter in reply to reject the request. Finally, the weights and measures case was discussed. The attending members conducted a thorough discussion, and the meeting adjourned at more than 7:00 PM.

Commercial Tail-End Finds Will Abolish Li and Use Fen

▲ Silver and Money Industries are in Contact

In Shanghai, the unit of calculation for the amount of money needed for commercial imports and exports is "fen" for Western merchants and "li" for Chinese merchants. The procedure is particularly cumbersome, but the habit is long-standing and unbreakable. It is now heard that the financial community has proposed that, starting from February 19th or March 1st of this year, following the example of Western merchants, the tail-end numbers of silver dollars will also be calculated in "fen." If there are "li" numbers below "fen," they will be rounded up or down using the rounding method (for example, four "li" will be deleted, and five "li" will be calculated as one "fen"). This proposal has been exchanged between the silver and money industries. If there are no other obstacles, it will be announced and implemented soon.

Responsibility for Commercial Firm's Letters, Seals, and Guarantees

▲ Commercial Firms and Their Shareholders and Owners Should Be Responsible

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, in order to explain the issue of responsibility for commercial firms' letters, seals, and guarantees on behalf of others, sent a letter to lawyer Liu Shifang yesterday, stating: I am replying directly. I received your letter stating that there are two views on the issue of the store owner's responsibility when a commercial firm's manager uses the firm's letters and seals to guarantee on behalf of others. One view is that the store owner is also fully responsible, and the other is that the store owner should not be responsible for matters handled by the manager. Each view has its own reasons, and you are instructed to interpret them. After investigating the business practices in the commercial world, the commercial firm's letters and seals represent the commercial firm. The status of a commercial firm is that of a legal person, and the organizers of the commercial firm are the shareholders or owners of the commercial firm. Therefore, for all matters, since the commercial firm's letters and seals have been affixed, the commercial firm is naturally directly responsible, and in practice, the shareholders or owners are indirectly responsible. Because the reason why others trust this seal is that the commercial firm is reliable, and whether the commercial firm is reliable or not depends solely on the credit of its shareholders or store owners. Therefore, the commercial firm's seal can provide guarantees for goods and money in commercial transactions. As for the managers and partners in the commercial firm, they are legally employees, and employees are responsible to the store owner. Therefore, as your letter states, those who use the commercial firm's letters and seals to guarantee on behalf of others are directly the commercial firm, and indirectly the shareholders or store owners of the commercial firm. It cannot be explained by whether they knew about it beforehand or not whether they are responsible or not. Assuming that this letter was indeed issued without the consent of the shareholders or store owners, or if it is stated in the commercial firm's agreement that the seal is not allowed to be used to guarantee on behalf of others (but this does not apply to matters within the scope of the store's business), the method is only to have the shareholders or store owners of the commercial firm first acknowledge this responsibility, and then have the shareholders or store owners order the sealers to bear all the responsibilities that should be borne. It is absolutely impossible to shirk responsibility to the sealers and unload all responsibility. A corresponding letter is replied, hoping that you will check and abide by it.

Announcement on Determining the Collection of Interest from Pawnshops

The Shanghai County Government issued an announcement yesterday, stating: I have received instructions from the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, stating: I have received instructions from the Provincial Government, stating: According to a report from the Construction Department, the amended Rules for Pawnshop Business in this province have been announced and implemented. Later, the Provincial Pawnshop Association submitted a report stating that Article 16 of the Rules stated that if it is more than one month to five days, half a month's interest will be charged; if it is more than fifteen days, one month's interest will be charged, etc. According to the interpretation of common laws and regulations, it seems that half a month's interest should be charged after five days, and one month's interest should be charged after fifteen days. Please interpret this to show caution, etc. After reporting, the Governor instructed to handle it in accordance with the Association's request, etc. After separately informing and announcing the relevant counties, it was recorded that in December of last year, pawnshop owners from various counties convened a meeting at the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce and publicly submitted a request to temporarily postpone the implementation of Article 16 of the Pawnshop Rules, etc. The Provincial Pawnshop Association also submitted the same request, and the Governor ordered that this case had been rejected in the previous report, etc., ordering to be informed. Now, county magistrates from Jinshan, Changshu, Wuxian, Taixing, Taixian, Chongming, Nanhui, Qingpu, and other counties have separately reported the previous situation. In addition to issuing separate instructions not to allow it, there is a sincere concern that pawnshop owners in various counties may make excuses to request postponement and not comply with the previous clause to calculate interest, which concerns the legal interests of the poor. It is proposed that the Governor instruct the county magistrates of the sixty-one counties to quickly comply and announce it to the public in order to benefit the poor and avoid delays, etc. After investigating this case, the pawnshop representatives from various counties, such as Cao Deliang, etc., submitted a request to temporarily postpone the implementation, which was decided by the 361st meeting of this government's committee not to allow it, and instructions were issued to notify all pawnshops to abide by it. Now, according to the previous situation, it is appropriate to order the department to quickly inform the counties and instruct the pawnshops under their jurisdiction to comply with it and announce it to the public. This order is given for this reason, and except for separate orders, it is appropriate to order the county magistrate to quickly instruct the pawnshops under their jurisdiction to comply with it and announce it to the public. This order is given for this reason. In addition to separate orders to comply with it, it is appropriate to announce it so that pawnshops and all kinds of people should comply with it and not violate it. This announcement is given for this reason.

A Monk's Medical Practice is Resented

▲ Life is Not Bad, with Rich Income

▲ Jealous Colleagues Gather to Extort Money

The monk Han Jiang, registered in Nantong, is quite knowledgeable in medicine and practices medicine at 27 Fenzhou Road, Yangshupu. He also gives medicine to the poor and sick. The nearby villagers in the area, who are concerned about collecting firewood, all come to his door for treatment. His life is not bad. Xie Dichen, a Jiangbei native in the area, also practices medicine, but his income is not as rich as Han Jiang's. Therefore, he turned from envy to jealousy. On the evening of the second day, Han Jiang had already gone to bed when he suddenly heard a knock. He ordered the porter to ask. The person outside said that a sick family had specially asked Han Jiang to make a house call. But listening carefully, it seemed that there was more than one person outside. Han Jiang was worried about an accident and said that if they really wanted to see a doctor, they should wait until the next morning. The people outside then began to scold him and knocked on the door more violently. He then ordered the porter to open the door, and saw Xie Dichen leading several people in, saying to Han Jiang, "We are colleagues, but you alone are making a huge profit. Now that the end of the year is approaching, it is difficult to survive. Allow us to borrow 1,000 gold coins, or don't blame us for not having the feelings of a colleague." Han Jiang refused, and Xie and his accomplices left angrily. At 9:00 AM the next morning, Han Jiang was hanging up his sign when Xie and his colleagues Xu Bohua and Li Yuanfang suddenly arrived again, still demanding 1,000 gold coins and preventing him from hanging up his sign, causing a disturbance for a long time before leaving at noon. They went again at the end of the day. If he didn't give them money, they would kill him in three days. During the argument, Han Jiang's maid, Yu Songshi, secretly exited from the back door and reported to the 2115th Huapu, saying that there was a robbery in her employer's house. The Huapu then reported to the police station by telephone, and sent detective Pang Ruiqing and a Western detective to rush to the scene. After investigation, it was confirmed that it was extortion rather than robbery, and the three, Xie, etc., were arrested. Yesterday, they were sent to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Feng Shide questioned them. Ru Baoyi, the police station's lawyer, stated that this matter was entirely caused by jealousy among colleagues and requested an investigation. Then, Han Jiang, his gatekeeper Yu Youshan, and his maid Yu Songshi, successively described the three times that the defendants had come to extort money. Questioning Xie, Xu, and Li, they all denied it. Judge Feng finished the questioning and ordered the defendants to be returned to prison to await a scheduled sentence.

A Punch Kills a Man

▲ The Result of Rickshaw Pullers Competing for Business

Wang Dalang, a native of Haimen Town west of Jiangwan Town, and his younger brother Wang Qilang, currently 20 years old, both earn a living pulling rickshaws. Around 4 PM the day before yesterday, Qilang rented a rickshaw from the rickshaw company opened by Li Yingxiang, a Hebei native, at that location. While touting for business along the way, he soon found a customer. As they were discussing the fare, a rickshaw pulled by Gu Gendi forcibly snatched the customer away. Qilang, extremely angry and unwilling to give up, stepped forward, hoping to retrieve the customer. Unexpectedly, Gu suddenly struck his waist with a powerful punch. A sound of "Ai yo" was heard, and Qilang fell to the ground, motionless. Gu, thinking he was faking it, ignored him and continued pushing the rickshaw. After a while, passersby noticed that he remained motionless for a long time, and upon approaching, they saw that his face was pale, and he was frothing at the mouth, on the verge of death. They quickly sent him back to the rickshaw company and called his elder brother, Dalang. He was still able to say that he had been beaten by Gu Gendi. Just as they were about to send him to the hospital for treatment, he died. Dalang, grieving deeply over his brother's tragic death, immediately reported to the Fifth Precinct of the Fifth Public Security Bureau, ordering the police to detain the murderer, Gu Gendi, and summon the rickshaw owner, Li Yingxiang. According to the elder brother of the deceased, his brother was about to get married next month, but now he has been beaten to death, and he demands justice. Gu Gendi, 22 years old, confessed that it was an accidental act and not intentional, pleading for leniency. Since the case involves a human life, besides ordering the local warden to report to the court for an autopsy, Gu and others will be sent to the Judicial Section for interrogation and handling.
