Local News Two

The Origin of the Heavy Fog in This Port

▲ Blown in from the Annam Region

For the past few days, there has been a heavy fog blanketing the area around the waterfront of Shanghai. The fog is particularly dense, making it impossible to see anything beyond a few yards. Foreign and coastal ships have been delaying their arrival in Shanghai to avoid the fog. For example, on the day before yesterday, only the Xinjiangtian and Ningxing vessels entered port. In the shipping industry, this has truly been unseen for many years. According to the Xujiahui Observatory, this fog was blown in from the Annam region, spreading along the coast and the Yangtze River basin. When it encountered the cold air of northern China, it became even denser. It is feared that it will not completely dissipate in the next day or two. What is even more strange is that since the fog descended, the weather has become noticeably warmer. Checking the weather on January 31st, the first day the fog was observed, the lowest temperature in this port was 40 degrees, and the highest was 48 degrees. On February 1st, the lowest increased to 41 degrees, and the highest rose to 54 degrees. On February 2nd, the fog became even heavier, and the temperature also increased, with the lowest increasing to 41.9 degrees and the highest reaching 53.6 degrees. The last two days have been even warmer. This kind of temperature is not common in late winter and early spring.

Du Miaojuan's Divorce Lawsuit

▲ Once Reached a Settlement Out of Court

▲ Cao Qinye Lacks Money to Cope

▲ Miaojuan Loves Her Three Children Dearly

▲ The Judge Earnestly Advises Reconciliation

▲ Having Borne One Son and Two Daughters Cao Rangzhi, who once served as the director of the Shatin Bureau, has a son named Qinye, currently 24 years old. He works in the accounting department of the Japanese-owned Gongda Spinning Factory. In the 14th year, he married Miaojuan, the daughter of physician Du Jingxian. They are the same age and have been married for six years, bearing two daughters and one son. One daughter is five years old, and the other is four years old. The son is only three years old. However, the couple's relationship has never been very harmonious, though not absolutely hostile, so they have managed to maintain it for several years.

▲ Filing for Divorce After Being Beaten It was not until February 1st of last year, after Ms. Du was beaten and injured, that they had a major falling out. She returned to her parents' home for medical treatment and filed a lawsuit in court. The matter was then settled through reconciliation. Now, due to unresolved issues, Ms. Du hired lawyer Xu Bingcheng to file a divorce lawsuit against Cao in the Special District Local Court, requesting a divorce decree, recovery of dowry, living expenses, and medical expenses. She also requested that the two daughters be returned to her custody, while the son would be raised by the defendant. This case was previously heard once by the Special District Court, which ordered them to attempt reconciliation out of court. Now, because reconciliation is difficult to achieve,

▲ Four Conditions for Reconciliation Therefore, at 10 AM yesterday morning, Judge Yang opened the tenth court to continue the hearing. The plaintiff, Du Miaojuan, and her lawyers, Du Lingjun and Xu Bingcheng, the defendant, Cao Qinye, and his lawyer, Qu Yue, were all present in court. After the trial began, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that the plaintiff had proposed the following conditions for reconciliation: (1) The defendant should apologize to the plaintiff; (2) The defendant should bear the medical expenses; (3) The defendant should be responsible for the children's education expenses; (4) The plaintiff's future livelihood should be guaranteed. If the defendant can fully fulfill these conditions, the couple's relationship can be restored, and they can continue to live together.

▲ The Judge Strongly Urges Reconciliation Judge Yang then questioned the defendant, Cao Qinye, stating that the plaintiff has now proposed conditions for reconciliation. Except for the second item, medical expenses of 1,200 yuan, the first item, an apology, is not a problem. For the third item, children's education, and the fourth item, future living expenses, since you are already living together as a couple, you should naturally be responsible. Therefore, if you can give the plaintiff 1,000 yuan now, you can reconcile. However, Cao stated that he works as an accountant in the factory and only earns 40 yuan per month, so he is unable to afford this large sum. Judge Yang also said that it is not difficult to borrow or gather 1,000 yuan from relatives and friends. Furthermore, since you are a couple, although the 1,000 yuan is given to the plaintiff, it still belongs to you in reality. You should know that if you proceed with the divorce, you will lose even more. Therefore, in the opinion of this court, reconciliation is still the best option. Cao stated that he is willing to reconcile, but he lacks the means. The plaintiff, Du Miaojuan, immediately stated that the defendant is not sincere about reconciliation. Judge Yang asked the plaintiff how much money she wants for items three and four. The plaintiff replied that she needs 200 yuan per month.

▲ The Defendant's Brother-in-Law's Statement Judge Yang then summoned the defendant's brother-in-law, Shao Zhongdao, for questioning. Shao stated that the defendant only earns a salary of just over 30 yuan per month at the factory. His father has already passed away, and he only has a stepmother at home. Although his father had some assets when he was alive, they have all been exhausted since his death. Now, not only is there no family property, but he also owes 8,800 yuan. He was also asked if he was present when the plaintiff and defendant fought. Shao replied that he was not present. He later heard that the defendant could not fall asleep, so he went to the study to read the newspaper, but he was refused entry to the room by the plaintiff, which led to the fight.

▲ Current Assets and Property Numbers Judge Yang asked Du Miaojuan if the defendant had any family property at all. Du replied that when she got married, she heard the matchmaker say that he had 100,000 to 200,000 yuan in family property. After marrying, she learned that the defendant had three properties near the Jinshenfu Road in the French Concession. When his father was alive, he also had cash deposits in the Shandong Bank. It is hard to believe that the defendant claims to be poor. After hearing the plaintiff's words, the defendant immediately said that he did own property on Jinshenfu Road, but he has already sold it all. As for the deposits in the Shandong Bank, they have long since vanished due to the bank's collapse. This can be proven by his brother-in-law, Shao Zhongdao. Du Miaojuan also stated that the defendant already earned 30 yuan per month when he entered the factory. Since then, he has received two pay raises each year. It has been six years, so he earns much more than 40 yuan.

▲ Willing to Dedicate All His Possessions At this point, Judge Cheng again strongly urged both parties. Cao replied that he is very grateful for the court's kindness, but he lacks the ability to come up with this sum of 1,000 yuan. Furthermore, since they were originally a couple, if they are sincere about reconciliation, why should they haggle over money? He also stated that he is now willing to give all of his monthly income to her for her use. In the future, if he can become wealthy, he can also completely hand it over to her for safekeeping. At this point, Judge Yang again questioned the plaintiff about the events of the beating and the medical certificate. He also asked Du Miaojuan how much alimony she wants. Ren replied 10,000 yuan, and claimed that the defendant has 100,000 to 200,000 yuan in family property. Asking for this amount is not excessive.

▲ Studying the Divorce Issue Judge Yang asked if she would not need to request living expenses if they reconciled. Du replied that it is necessary. He also asked Cao Qinye if he is willing to divorce, since the plaintiff has been like this. Cao replied that he is not willing. He was asked again if he is not willing to divorce, how much money he is willing to give the plaintiff. Cao still replied that he has no money. The plaintiff's lawyer stood up and stated that when the two sides discussed the divorce terms the other day, the plaintiff requested 10,000 yuan in alimony, and the defendant requested a reduction. It can be seen that the defendant is neither sincere about reconciliation nor absolutely without money. Judge Cheng asked Cao Qinye if this was the case. Cao replied that they are extorting him, asking for 12,000 yuan. He also asked Shao Zhongdao if he could assist in negotiating the divorce terms. Shao replied that he cannot assist and must consult his stepmother before proceeding.

▲ Enduring Six Years of Suffering At this point, the defendant's lawyer, Qu Yue, strongly urged both parties to reconcile, saying that the conditions are not a major problem. As for the amount of compensation for medical expenses, the defendant can set the amount himself. The method could be to pay in installments. Judge Yang also said that if you consider the children, it is best not to divorce. Du Miaojuan replied that she is very grateful for the court's intention. It was originally for the sake of the children that she was able to swallow her anger and endure six years of suffering. However, Cao Qinye not only disregarded the feelings of the children but also wanted to take her life, so she filed this divorce lawsuit. Judge Yang then announced that the case cannot be reconciled at this time and must be adjourned until the actual situation of the defendant's family circumstances is investigated and witnesses are summoned, after which arguments will begin. He then adjourned the court.

Robbery on Ningbo Road

▲ Yongheng Money Shop Robbed Upon Leaving

▲ Three Hundred Yuan Retained, Five Thousand Yuan Snatched

A branch of the Yongheng Bank on Ningbo Road was sending 5,300 yuan in cash to Xingren Lane on the same road yesterday morning. As they were walking west on Shandong Road, three thugs suddenly appeared, blocking the way and robbing 5,000 yuan in cash. The branch staff staggered back to the bank. Aside from crying, there was nothing they could do. Near Happiness Sui Lane, workers were repairing telephones. Seeing the righteousness of the situation, they bravely ran to the police station to report the incident. Upon learning of the incident, the patrolmen immediately pursued the suspects westward. At the intersection of Henan Road, one robber was arrested. He opened fire, was injured, and was captured. The remaining robbers fled with the stolen money, disappearing like yellow cranes. Robberies in broad daylight are not uncommon, but Ningbo Road is an area with many money shops and banks, where security is usually tight. The robbery of a large sum of money on the street and the opening of fire by the police are unprecedented events since the New Year.

▲ Five Thousand Yuan in Banknotes Lightly Parted Between Ningbo Road and Tianjin Road, money shops and banks stand side by side, holding a portion of the Shanghai financial world's power. As the old lunar year draws to a close, businesses are accustomed to settling accounts and collecting money, doing so far more than usual. Yesterday morning around 9:30, the Shanghai Yongheng Bank at No. 86 Ningbo Road was sending 5,300 yuan to a certain shop in Xingren Lane on the same road at their request. Yongheng Bank employees thought that Xingren Lane was close at hand, within sight, and that the sum was not huge, so one person could handle it. Therefore, they ordered branch employee Zhou Bingchen to deliver it alone. However, for the sake of caution, the 5,300 yuan in banknotes was divided into two batches. A small sum of 300 yuan was hidden in his pocket, while the large sum of 5,000 yuan was wrapped in newspaper and held in his hand. To conceal it from prying eyes, they had to use this method of prioritizing the lesser sum. As soon as he left the branch, disaster struck. About thirty or forty steps eastward, three people suddenly emerged. Two people crowded Zhou's shoulders, while one robber stood in front, making a slight bow, and the loud pistol was already pressed against Zhou's chest. Poor Zhou, barely able to regain his composure, watched the banknotes disappear. The robbers were indeed after the 5,000 yuan in the newspaper.

▲ The View from the Top of the Hundred-Foot Pole In the past, Ningbo Road had narrow streets and poor conditions. Today, the area east of Henan Road is lined with grand bank buildings, creating a new atmosphere. Even the Fusuinong and other lanes opposite the Yongheng Bank west of Shandong Road have new, towering buildings, newly renovated. However, because construction has not been long underway, completion is slow, and the relocation of utility poles along the road is a recent event. Because of the relocation of telephone poles at the entrance of Fusu Lane, yesterday there were many workers from the telephone company repairing wires there. From the top of the hundred-foot pole, the ground below is clearly visible. Among them, a certain Mr. Jia witnessed the three robbers attacking Zhou Bingchen in great detail because they were not far away. For a moment, driven by righteous indignation, he roared like a lion and strode forward, following behind the robbers to the intersection of Henan Road, where he informed the patrol police. Therefore, the gun fired, and the robbers were captured. What a pity that the 5,000 yuan in banknotes had already drifted away with the robbers in the gunpowder smoke.

▲ Bullets Fired, Robbers' Pockets Empty After the robbery of the large sum of cash, Zhou Bingchen, due to excessive fright and mental confusion, immediately ran back to the bank. Reaching the steps, he was already weeping with his face covered. When people asked him, he did not answer in detail, so the Yongheng Bank employees initially did not know what had happened to this branch employee. It was not until the patrolmen chased the robbers and passersby shouted that they learned the 5,000 yuan in banknotes had fallen into the hands of the robbers. After receiving the report, the patrol police at the intersection of Henan Road pursued the three robbers. The robbers fled westward and made a gesture of reaching into their pockets for a gun. To preempt them, the police immediately fired their guns, about three shots, hitting two of them. One robber immediately fell to the ground. At this time, many Chinese policemen had already surrounded and assisted. Since each lane and bank on Ningbo Road has armed guards, they rushed out to help when they heard the gunshots. In no time, the Central Police Station also received the news and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to search the scene and arrest the robbers. As if reaching into a bag, the injured robber's pockets were empty. Aside from the pistol weapon, there was nothing else. The so-called 5,000 yuan was nowhere to be found after a thorough search.

▲ Branch Employee Kept Money Safe in His Pocket The injured robber was sent to the Tongren Hospital in a police car for emergency treatment. He claimed to be surnamed Lin, named Dejing, 27 years old, from Jiangbei. He had two gunshot wounds on his body, one in the buttocks and one in the head. Later, this robber was transferred to the Public Concession Hospital. Detectives also discovered that his accomplices lived in the Central Hotel, so they rushed there and arrested two male and one female suspects. As for Zhou Bingchen, the Yongheng Bank branch employee, holding the 300 yuan in banknotes that remained in his pocket, he could not help but reflect on his pain, but as a survivor of the robbery, unharmed, he could be considered very lucky.

Cause of the Salty Taste of Zhabei Tap Water

▲ Does Not Harm Health

Recently, the tap water in Zhabei has tasted slightly salty. When asked about this by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, it was said that the reason is that the water plant is located downstream of the Huangpu River, and the Yangtze River's water level is low, making it easier for the sea tide to enter. The water plant has taken precautions, and the chemists test the mixed water every half hour. They only turn on the machines to draw water when the salt content is low. However, the tides have been very strong in recent days. The chloride content in the mixed water in the Huangpu River is at most over two thousand three hundred, and the average is about five hundred parts per million. However, this salty taste does not harm health and is perfectly safe to use. In a day or two, after the tide passes, it will return to its original state.

Rotary Club Special Commissioner David Heath Arrives in Shanghai

▲ Will Travel to North China

David Heath, the Honorary Commissioner of the International Rotary Club, has arrived in Shanghai with his wife and daughter, Mijiaoli, and several others. They are staying at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund. Twenty-six years ago, Mr. Heath was the US Consul General in Shanghai, handling diplomatic affairs in the Far East for a total of eight years. He recently organized a Rotary branch in Hong Kong. On the opening day, there were a total of more than 130 members. It is said that Mr. Heath will travel to North China via the Jinpu Railway within this week.

Eight Immortals Bridge Market Holds Daily Lottery for Locations

▲ The Chinese Ratepayers Association Sends Personnel to Supervise the Lottery

▲ Small Vendor Representatives Unexpectedly Fail to be Selected

The stall locations at the Eight Immortals Bridge Market in the French Concession have been assigned by lottery in recent days. During the lottery, to prevent impersonation or fraud, the French Municipal Council specially arranged for the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association to send personnel to supervise. Therefore, the Association specially sent committee member Cheng Zhusun, carrying the vendor registration forms, to verify with the Municipal Council that there were no errors. The lottery was held at 2 PM on the afternoons of the day before yesterday and yesterday. When the vendors entered, vendor representatives Chen Yunqing, Wei Azhang, Zhang Chuanyan, Zhu Yuxing, Yu Ade, and others, together with Municipal Council personnel, inspected the permits at the door to ensure that the names matched before allowing entry. Therefore, the lottery method was very fair, and each lottery number was inspected by vendor representatives, Association committee member Cheng, and others before being inserted into the lottery drum, and then the lottery was drawn separately. Unexpectedly, as a result of the lottery, the representatives who had worked hard to advocate for all the vendors were not selected. The stall locations they received were all of the worst quality. For example, Chen Achang (one of the representatives) received a location next to the public toilet. In disappointment, he was willing to sacrifice his permit and destroyed it himself. All the vendors witnessed this and praised the representatives for handling matters fairly. It is said that they will have special measures to reward Mr. Chen.

Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau Urges the Relocation of Dock Coal and Charcoal Shops

▲ To Build Dock Public Toilets

There are coal and charcoal shops such as Gonghexing, Hongji, and Qiaji on the banks of docks with numbers 5, 6, and 7 in South Shanghai, which store coal and charcoal. Due to excessive loads, the banks are in danger. Furthermore, the piled coal and charcoal, as tall as the buildings, affects the appearance and fire safety of the docks. After the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau took over the docks, it was limited to before January 15th, all of which were to be relocated. After the merchants expressed their difficulties, the extension was extended to January 27th. On this day, the merchants relocated all the piled coal and charcoal in heavy snow. The Engineering Bureau completely demolished the dilapidated wooden houses in the area, creating a new look. In addition, the original dock public toilets were insufficient and poorly equipped. The surroundings of the toilets reeked. The former Port Authority had previously worked with the Health Bureau to survey the locations for additional public toilets, ordering the cleaning contractor to handle them, but no construction was started. The Public Utilities Bureau believes that the cleanliness of the docks is related to the appearance of the city for both Chinese and foreigners and cannot be ignored. It has consulted with the Health Bureau, ordering the cleaning contractor to build new-style public toilets with pumping equipment. On January 29th, it sent representatives from the Health, Public Security, Land, and Engineering Bureaus to survey six locations, including docks 1, 3, 10, and 15 and the north ends of the Dachuzhan and Wanyu docks, to build public toilets, with docks 1 and 3 being the first to be built.

Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau Employee Thrift Savings Measures

▲ Money Deposited in the Shanghai Municipal Bank

▲ Implemented Starting in January

To promote thrift among employees and in view of the poor environment in Shanghai, where young people with unstable minds are particularly vulnerable to falling into depravity, the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau has formulated employee thrift savings measures. It was approved at the 160th Bureau Affairs Meeting and submitted to the Municipal Government for review and filing. It was specially discussed and resolved by the Municipal Council, and the Bureau will first conduct a trial run for half a year to observe the effectiveness. The measures are mandatory for single employees and voluntary for non-single employees and have been implemented since January of this year. A total of 25 single employees have saved 272.50 yuan, and 12 non-single employees have saved 144.50 yuan. In addition, one public servant has also saved 5 yuan. In total, 38 people have saved 422 yuan. The money is entrusted to the Municipal Bank for safekeeping because its interest rate is higher than other banks.

Western Clothing Industry Asks for a Reduction in Business Tax

The Shanghai Western Clothing Industry Association yesterday sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Tax Regulations Research Committee, saying: "Respectfully, for the matter of requesting a submission to the authorities of Beijing, provinces, and cities, please allow a reduction of business tax rate for the Western clothing and woolen industry. The National Government abolished the likin tax, originally to eliminate harmful commercial practices and bad governance. The provinces use business tax to offset the likin tax revenue. Merchants and citizens, in order to respect the central government's regulations, should strive to pay. However, the determination of the business tax rate, if too high or too low, will inevitably become an exorbitant tax, which merchants and citizens find difficult to bear. According to the Outline for the Collection of Business Tax by the Provinces promulgated by the National Government, the collection of business tax should not exceed two per thousand. Western clothing and woolens are at the head of the four essentials of human life. Although they mostly involve the sale of foreign goods, woolens are daily necessities and cannot be compared to luxury goods. At this time when there are no comparable domestic substitutes and there is no need for bans, Western clothing is related to international affairs. The National Dress Code does not prohibit it, so it is needed just like ordinary secondhand clothing, and cannot be regarded as a luxury item or in need of bans. The amount of business tax collected from our industry does not comply with Article 4 of the Outline. Furthermore, the raw materials of ordinary secondhand clothing are not necessarily all domestic products, and the Western clothing industry is striving to use domestic products, so the amount of business tax collected from our industry does not comply with Article 7 of the supplementary measures to the Outline. Moreover, the business profits of our industry are extremely small. Since the increase in tariffs due to the preciousness of gold and the cheapness of silver, it has been difficult to maintain. If the current collection method of Jiangsu Province must be implemented, then the meager profits of our industry's hard work each year will be completely paid to business tax, which is still not enough. In two or three years, they will inevitably be bankrupted, and the livelihoods of all the industry's workers will also be cut off. The dangerous future is unthinkable. Concerning the lives of the people, the peace of society, we must sincerely ask your committee to submit a request to the authorities, please reduce the business tax rate for the Western clothing and woolen industry to at most two per thousand, in order to maintain people's livelihood and benefit commercial transportation. This is the purpose of this letter."

Opening Date for the Lu Yifang Appeal Case

▲ 2 PM on the Sixth

Actress Hu Die of the Star Film Company had a problem with her fiancé, Lin Xuehuai, regarding the termination of their engagement. Because the Sanri Daily published an article entitled "Hu Lin Divorce Record," which stated that Hu had entered the red dust and depended on people to be a small star, Hu believed that the newspaper intentionally defamed her reputation and hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to send a letter of correction. After the correction, the newspaper published a photo of the company's male actor, Zhu Fei, with a caption "A Key Figure in the Xue Die Divorce." Hu even more believed that it was deliberately destroying her reputation and filed a criminal self-accusation with the Special District Court. On the afternoon of December 29th last year, after Judge Feng tried the case, he immediately sentenced Lu Yifang to damage to another person's reputation and fined him 300 yuan. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, two yuan will be deducted for each day. Lu Yifang declared in court that he did not accept the appeal. It is now known that Lu has hired another lawyer, Jiang Yiping, to represent him. The case is scheduled to open at 2 PM on the sixth, and there will be another eloquent debate at that time.

Russian Accused of Opening Gambling Den Case Concludes Debate

▲ Sentencing set for next Wednesday

The case of Gao Laisi Regaof, Chairman of the Russian Military Association, accusing Ai Haiyingpeng Fan Chelin of embezzling funds from the association to open a gambling den, was heard yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM by Judge Cheng Shangfeng in the Fifth Court. Both defendants and their representing lawyers were present in court. After Judge Cheng ascended the bench, the plaintiff's lawyer, Qiu Fen,

Page 16

submitted a piece of evidence to Judge Cheng to question Fan Chelin. (The evidence was a contract between Fan Chelin and Bao Men for the distribution of commissions.) The judge asked Fan Chelin whether the signature on the contract was indeed his. Fan answered that it was. The judge asked, "Who made the contract?" Fan answered that he did not know. The judge then asked, "If you didn't know, why did you sign it?" Fan answered, "I was in a position of arbitration, so I signed it." After Judge Cheng questioned this far, he announced the start of the debate. After plaintiff's lawyer Qiu, and defendant's lawyer Wei, debated the three items of (1) opening a gambling den, (2) embezzling from the association, and (3) making false accusations, Judge Cheng asked the plaintiff if they had anything to add. The plaintiff then stated, "(1) I did not use a handgun to threaten him, (2) Ai Haiyingpeng is merely the facade, and Fan Chelin is the mastermind, (3) the military association must publish various military books and reports every month, and this matter should not be allowed to stop it. At the same time, since this association was originally a military association, opening a gambling den should be prohibited." Judge Cheng then asked Ai Haiyingpeng if he had anything to add. Ai then stated, "I am the manager of the association. Matters within the association cannot be asked of me. It is like a bank collapsing; you should ask the owner, not the manager." Fan Chelin stated, "I do not know about this matter. I only acted as a guarantor on the contract, and I do not know anything else." Judge Cheng then announced the conclusion of the debate on the case and set the sentencing for 2:00 PM next Wednesday. The defendants, Ai Haiyingpeng and Fan Chelin, and the counter-defendant, Gao Laisi Regaof, were each released on bail of a shop guarantee or 1,000 yuan in cash before leaving the court.

Ka Ming Li Robbery Case Solved

▲ More than half of the stolen goods have been recovered

On the 24th of last month, the home of Qian Meiting, a Ningbo jeweler at No. 25 Kai Ming Li, Nine Acres, South City, was robbed of a large amount of jewelry and diamonds by violent thieves, and one Zhu Rufa was shot and wounded. Details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the case was solved the day before yesterday. Although there were brief reports in the newspapers, due to the investigation, it was inconvenient to disclose all the details. It is now learned that the case has been completely solved, and more than half of the stolen goods have been recovered. The detailed process is described below. After the case occurred, Yuan Liang, the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, immediately instructed the district offices and teams to solve the case, recover the stolen goods, and arrest the real thieves within a time limit. After receiving the instruction, Lu Ying, the head of the Detective Squad, immediately summoned all the lead detectives for a briefing and supervised them to go to various entertainment venues and hotels in the British and French Concessions for secret investigations. Until the 29th of last month, the leader Qi Haitian reported that the ringleader of the robbery, nicknamed "Little Guangdong" (Wu Chaofang, also known as "Little Ya"), was hiding at No. 3 Jinxiu Fang, Huanghe Road, French Concession. After receiving the report, Captain Lu immediately dispatched detectives Zhang Guangsen, Miao Jinhai, Zhou Peisan, Ling Tianpeng, Yan Zhuming, Zhang Yingpin, etc., together with Chinese and foreign detectives from the French Police Department, to disguise and wait at the location. At around 3:00 PM on the 30th, they saw five thieves coming from outside and entering the house at No. 3. Seeing that the thieves had entered the house, Qi and the others bravely stepped forward and completely captured the five thieves. They found a diamond-encrusted jade duck egg ring in the house. The five thieves then led them to the Zhongxing Hotel on Xiafei Road, as well as No. 17 on that road, and the Anle Hotel and Nanjing Hotel on Caishi Street, where they arrested Chen Jinsheng, Lu Heshang, and Zhu Genbao. They also seized eleven diamonds. Lu Heshang and Chen Jinsheng then confessed that their accomplice, Liu Guisheng, was hiding at No. 692 Fangbang Road. They arrested Liu and seized seven bullets. There are still accomplices at large, and the investigation is continuing to prevent any from escaping.

Ministry Orders Social Bureau to Maintain the Interests of Depositors of the Day and Night Bank

Regarding the case of the Shanghai Great World Amusement Savings Department's Day and Night Bank suspending operations and being liquidated, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce received a petition from the bank's creditors in the name of the Creditors' Temporary Committee, requesting that their interests be maintained. The ministry has again ordered the Shanghai Social Bureau to expedite the liquidation and hold those with unlimited liability accountable. The official order is recorded below: Industrial and Commercial Ministry Order No. 890, to be followed: Received a telegram from the Shanghai Great World Amusement Savings Department Day and Night Bank creditors in the name of the Creditors' Temporary Committee stating that, "After the death of Shanghai merchant Huang Chu Jiu, his relatives and friends organized a post-mortem committee to maintain his remaining businesses, such as real estate, tobacco, pharmacies, native products, cinemas, etc., as usual. However, they declared the Shanghai Day and Night Bank and the Great World Amusement Savings Department to be under liquidation. So far, there has been no concrete action, causing the rights of thousands of depositors to waver, feeling deeply distressed and miserable beyond words. We have investigated that in the banking industry, operating savings businesses, it is customary for the board of directors and important officers to bear unlimited liability. Moreover, this department was originally a company with unlimited liability. Even if all of Huang's businesses were declared bankrupt, the bank and the department should still repay all depositors' principal and interest in full. Furthermore, since all other businesses are being maintained, the rights of the bank and the department's creditors should be repaid earlier. We implore your ministry to consider that these thousands of depositors are all poor commoners, with only a few thousand or hundreds of yuan each, and as little as dozens or a few yuan, mostly the small amount of sweat and toil accumulated over time by hard work and thrift. Once they suffer losses, their lives and livelihoods are in danger. The weeping and wailing of the elderly and the cries of shop assistants and laborers in front of the bank, the department, and Huang's residence every day are evidence that the rights of these two parts have a great impact on the economy of Shanghai's common people. We beg your ministry to promptly order the Shanghai Municipal Government's Social Bureau to uphold justice and order the post-mortem committee to clear the principal and interest of the bank and the department's creditors in the shortest possible time to protect the rights of creditors and appease the public." We have investigated that this case was previously ordered by the ministry to be handled carefully, as it concerned social finance, and not to be handled according to the method of a limited liability company. Now, according to the previous situation, we hereby order the bureau to expedite the liquidation, holding those with unlimited liability accountable to avoid losses for depositors and maintain social finance. This order.

Two-Year-Old Boy Missing from Qiao Jia Road

Kidnappers frequently lurk on the streets of South City, specializing in luring and abducting young boys and girls. It is said that these kidnappers have organized an organization, where they change the children's names, teach them how to address them, and once the training is complete, sell them to other places for profit. Therefore, in recent days, there have been numerous cases of children being abducted and lost, and their families are seen wandering around the city, carrying foot warmer lids and calling out their names in the streets. It is now reported that a two-year-old boy from the family surnamed Mou, residing at a certain address on Qiao Jia Road, Xiaonanmen, was taken by his nanny for a stroll outside the door yesterday morning around 9:00 AM. The nanny then went upstairs to get something, and when she came downstairs, the child had suddenly disappeared. They immediately searched everywhere but could not find him. It is suspected that he was also abducted. After the child's parents learned of this, they cried all day and reported the matter to the police for investigation. It is not known whether the child can be recovered.

Vocational Association of the YWCA

The YWCA in this city, in view of the lack of group life and mutual assistance opportunities for working women in Shanghai, has established a vocational women's association. Yesterday afternoon at 7:00 PM, it invited working women from all walks of life to hold the second preparatory meeting at the association's location on Nanjing Road. About twenty guests attended the meeting. The meeting ended at 10:00 PM with a meal. The association is scheduled to hold the third discussion meeting at the association's location at 6:00 PM on Tuesday, the 10th of this month, and to elect official committee members, etc. Dinner will be prepared at that time to welcome working women from all walks of life to join.

News of the Engineering Society Seeking Talents

The Chinese Engineering Society is the only organization composed of engineers in our country. Since its establishment, it has gained a reputation for its service to construction and academic research. In particular, the Employment Introduction Committee organized by the society is the most important work. Therefore, many people from various places entrust the society to hire talents. In the past, it was only for the adjustment of employment for the society's members, and it never sought applications from the outside world, so few people knew about it. Recently, the society's members have all had fairly stable positions, but there are still many requests from various places to hire talents on their behalf, resulting in a situation where supply cannot meet demand. It is now learned that there are still no applicants for the request letters received by the society, including the following three places: (1) A long-distance bus company in Shanghai needs an engineer to manage the entire road, who must be young, energetic, and not afraid of hard work. The salary is negotiable. (2) A university in Hunan needs a professor of mathematics and physics, who must be a graduate of a European or American university, have teaching experience, and be able to use English textbooks. The monthly salary is 260 yuan. (3) A certain place needs a chemical engineering expert, who must analyze minerals monthly and focus on the research of rare minerals, and must be a graduate of a foreign engineering school to be qualified. The salary is very generous. If any of the readers are interested, please contact the society directly at No. 47 Ningbo Road, Shanghai. Those seeking engineering talents can also send a letter to the society for registration, so that they can be contacted when there is a suitable opportunity in the future. If engineering institutions in various places need to hire engineering talents, they can also inform the society, and the society will surely give a satisfactory reply.

News from Various Labor Unions

The Candle Industry Union convened a general meeting of members yesterday, with more than ninety people in attendance. Chairman Chen Zenghao reported on the ten newly revised conditions, which were satisfactory to the members and were passed. It was resolved that the rest days during night work would remain the same, and the working hours would be limited to ten hours. Overtime would be punished according to the old rules, and personnel would be appointed to be responsible for inspection. The meeting ended with a discussion of the membership fee issue.

▲The Wharf Workers' Union held its sixty-seventh standing committee meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. Chairman Chen Haiqiu conducted the ceremony as usual and gave a report. The following was discussed: (1) Liu Defu reported that Yan Zhirong, an executive committee member of the Second District, was falsely accused by Chen Rongzhao and detained by the police station and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. A request was made to prove his release. It was resolved to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau requesting his release. (2) Wu Jiaze, a standing committee member of the union, previously requested that Gan Xinmin be temporarily appointed as his replacement due to busy work. Now that Gan is unwell, what should be done? It was resolved to send a letter requesting Comrade Wu to cancel his leave immediately. (3) Feng Bingsheng, a representative of the China Merchants Bureau wharf workers, reported that someone had embezzled subsidies and requested that they be distributed equally. It was resolved that the union had summoned both parties to resolve the issue peacefully. (4) The union, by the previous joint meeting of various wharfs, decided to organize an economic custody committee. Jia Boxin, Li Yan, Wu Anxiang, Chen Zhenyu, Chen Xichang, Bai Xiaolan, and Peng Desheng were publicly recommended by each wharf as members of the custody economic committee, and Jia Boxin was elected as the director. The inauguration ceremony is scheduled to be held at the union at 10:00 AM on the 5th of this month. A report will be submitted to the Civil Training Association for filing. (5) The union's economic custody committee has been organized and established. All arrears from the wharfs must be paid in full within this week to clear the procedures.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky was cloudy and relatively cold, with local rain or fog in some areas, but it was gradually clearing. There was snow and strong northerly winds on the Shandong coast. There was a cyclone in the Yellow Sea, Korea, and the East China Sea due to the rain and a low-pressure center moving in the east-northeast direction. Also, in the twenty-four hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 54.0 degrees and the lowest was 46.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 45.7 degrees and the lowest was 38.3 degrees.
